78th Meeting of the Executive Yuan 65

The 78th meeting of the Executive Yuan was held on the 15th. Tan Yankai, Sun Ke, Wang Zhengting, Jiang Menglin, Liu Ruiheng, and Wang Boqun attended. Zheng Hongnian, Chen Yi, Zhang Wohua, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Yu, and Zeng Yangfu were present as observers. Tan Yankai chaired the meeting. Matters discussed: (1) Education Minister Jiang Menglin proposed that the 328,000 yuan in temporary fees requested by the Beiyang Institute of Technology in Tianjin be allocated appropriately, and that the institute's recurring expenses be approved and determined according to the original budget of 276,000 yuan for the 19th fiscal year reviewed by the ministry, without further reduction, in order to maintain the institute. Resolution: The temporary fees will be allocated by the Ministry of Education in consultation with the Russian Fund Committee, and the recurring expenses will be allocated by the Ministry of Finance in accordance with the amount of 276,000 yuan determined by the ministry. (2) Minister of Industry and Commerce Kong Xiangxi reported that he was instructed to review the case of whether the time for shop employees to join or leave employment could be changed to the Gregorian calendar as the standard. In accordance with the investigation, the customs of various industries and professions for shop employees to join or leave employment are different. It seems that it is still permissible to temporarily follow the old customs of various places and industries, and there is no need to stipulate a uniform date. However, since it has been clearly ordered that the Gregorian calendar be used for merchants' accounts, private contracts, and all documents and books, the old time for these shop employees to join or leave employment should be uniformly changed to the Gregorian calendar to comply with the law. Resolution: Approved according to the ministry's deliberation. (3) The Hankou Municipal Government reported that it had changed Hante City to Hankou City in compliance with the order, and requested that the various bureau chiefs and personnel recommended by the government be appointed in accordance with the newly formulated municipal organization law, immediately revoked, and reappointed. Resolution: Forwarded to the National Government for reappointment. (4) The Navy Department requested the appointment of Cheng Meixian, former deputy captain of the Yingrui warship, as the major staff officer of the Navy Torpedo Guerrilla Team. Resolution: Forwarded to the National Government for appointment. (5) The Zhejiang Provincial Government reported that Lou Zhaojian, secretary of the Secretariat of the Provincial Government, had requested to resign, and Liu Shixin would succeed him in the vacancy. Resolution: Approved and forwarded. (6) The Hunan Provincial Government reported that Wang Hanchuan, the second section chief of the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government, had been assigned to another position, and requested that Hu Nianseng be appointed to succeed him. Resolution: Approved and forwarded.

Central Army Repels Qufu and Yanzhou Jin Army 66

Jin Army Retreats to Gather at Nanyi and Ningyang

Xuzhou Communication: News from the Tianjin-Pukou Front. Recently, the Jin army, including the troops of Chuan Zuoyi, Li Shengda, and Zhang Huizhao, attacked the vicinity of Yanzhou and Qufu. They were all repelled by the Central Army. The Jin army also attacked Pan City in Qufu and was repelled by the defending troops. The Jin army in Nanxingbu and Xinzhuang south of Qufu has retreated to the area around the Confucius Forest Academy in Qufu. The Central Air Force has also been heading north in batches to bomb the Jin army. According to road news today (13th), the vanguard of the Central Army's flanking troops has broken through Qufu and is approaching Nanyi. The Jin army is retreating from the vicinity of Yanzhou and Qufu to gather at Nanyi and Ningyang. At the same time, the Central Army in western Shandong is also making a surprise move north. It is expected that there will be fierce fighting on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway and in western Shandong within two or three days. Currently, northbound passenger trains still reach Lincheng, and military trains can reach north of Zou County, and transportation is very smooth. (13th)

Zhang Xueliang's Representative Gao Shengyue and Others Arrive in Hankou 67

He Chengjun's representative, Gu Gengye, also arrives in Hankou. Correspondence from the Third Army Corps Commander, He Chengjun, previously sent his confidential secretary, Gu Gengye, to Liaoning to discuss military affairs with Zhang Xueliang, the Commander of the Northeast Border Defense, and to negotiate all matters. After arriving in Liaoning, Mr. Gu met with Mr. Zhang several times and negotiated everything. He had already reported to Commander He via telegram. At that time, the National Government specially appointed Mr. Zhang as the Deputy Commander of the Army, Navy, and Air Force. Mr. Zhang believed that it was necessary to contact the authorities here at any time, and he also sent Major General Gao Shengyue, Lieutenant Colonel Liu Tongke, Major Cai Zhifang, etc., to Hankou with Mr. Gu. They departed from Shenyang on the 4th of this month, first went to Huludao to meet with Mr. Zhang and ask for instructions on everything, then transferred by ship to Shanghai, and arrived in Hankou on the 12th by the Yushun steamboat. They arrived at 7 p.m. on the 14th and stayed at the Taotao Hotel. He's representative, Gu Gengye, returned to the Third Army Corps headquarters' garrison office to rest. After the reporter arrived at the residence of Mr. Gao, he immediately drove to visit him. According to him, Commander Zhang has always been consistent in supporting the Central Government and cherishing peace. The current situation in China is such that unification cannot be hoped for without supporting the Central Government, and survival cannot be achieved without stopping disputes and resisting foreign aggression. Commander Zhang will base his advocacy on this, telegraphing Yan Xishan and Feng Yuxiang to persuade them to cease fighting and fulfill the previous agreement to go abroad, so as to avoid the scourge of war and the suffering of the people, etc. Gu Gengye also said that this time, he was ordered to go to Liaoning, and the negotiation was extremely successful. Commander Zhang is now in Huludao and will return to Liaoning Ning to officially assume his new position as Deputy Commander of the Army, Navy, and Air Force. As for the military affairs of the Northeast, Mr. Zhang had already made arrangements. If Yan and Feng still dare to go their own way, troops will be sent to suppress them, etc. It is heard that Gao Shengyue is Mr. Zhang's official representative, and Liu Tongke and Cai Zhifang are military liaison officers. They plan to go to the headquarters in the morning of the 15th to pay their respects to He Yingqin, and on the 16th they will go to Luohe to pay their respects to He Chengjun to report everything in person. Whether they will be stationed in Hankou or at the front is yet to be decided. He's representative, Gu Gengye, will also go to the front to report on the negotiations with Mr. Zhang.

(July 14)

Hua Jueming Discusses the War Situation on All Fronts and the Political Affairs of Hubei 68

Hankou Correspondence: Hua Jueming, Secretary-General of the Third Army Corps Headquarters and Secretary-General of the Hubei Provincial Government, followed He Chengjun to the front, and was recently ordered to return to Hankou to discuss important matters with Wu Xingya, the Acting Chairman of the Provincial Government. The reporter met him at a certain place yesterday. According to him, the war situation on all fronts and the recent political situation in Hubei Province are very detailed. His words are recorded as follows:

On the Ping-Han Railway front, after the enemy's main force, Zhang Weixi's troops, were defeated by the Central Army, Feng retreated to the vicinity of Xuchang. The Central Army repeatedly challenged and lured the enemy into an ambush. In recent days, the enemy's elite troops have suffered heavy losses. The Battle of Maleji was particularly devastating. It is estimated that after three nights of fierce fighting, more than 800 enemy soldiers were killed, more than 1,000 were captured, more than 2,000 rifles were seized, dozens of machine guns, and more than 40 mortars. Commander He was at the front with Xu Yuanquan, Xiao Zhichu, Hao Menglin, Yang Hucheng, and other generals to discuss the strategy of attack, which has already been decided. There will definitely be progress within a few days. Chief of Staff Chen Guangzu recently received an order from Commander-in-Chief Chiang to personally inspect the front line by plane. It is reported that the Central Army at the front is in extremely high spirits, and the enemy troops have no will to fight. In the shortest possible time, Xuchang and Zhengzhou should be completely recovered. On the Jinpu Railway front, after the Central Army captured Dawenkou, it advanced rapidly towards Tai'an. The Jin troops Feng Pengzhu and Chuan Zuoyi's troops have been surrounded. After they are eliminated, they should drive straight in. The Longhai Railway front, which connects with the Jinpu and Ping-Han Railway lines, is also making steady progress. It will soon be possible to directly attack Kaifeng. On the Hunan front, Zhang Guigui's troops were relentlessly pursued and severely attacked by the Central Army, and suffered heavy losses. Yongzhou and Quanzhou were successively occupied by the Central Army. The enemy's Independent Third Regiment, about 1,000 people, completely surrendered. They are now fleeing to Guilin, and the Central Army is pursuing them in victory. On the northern Hubei front, the enemy's Liu Ruming's troops previously invaded Laohekou in Guanghua. They were jointly repelled by the 51st Division Fan Shisheng and the Independent First Brigade Xu Dezu directly under the Third Army Corps. They fled to the Zhangjiadian area and were intercepted by Army Commander Yang Hucheng, and have been surrounded and disarmed.

As for the political affairs of Hubei Province, there are currently two things that can be reported: one is the scheduled establishment of the new budget meeting, and the other is the preparation and commencement of the four yarn and hemp bureaus. It is understood that the Provincial Government previously discussed and decided on the budget committee for the 19th year of the province, and also formed an organization of all committee members. Zhang, the Director of Finance, also submitted the opinion book on the budget for the 19th year of revenue and expenditure to the 35th meeting of the Provincial Government, which was decided and handed over to the Budget Committee. The committee decided to establish it on the 16th. Regarding opinions on the budget book, such as streamlining agencies, reducing expenses, eliminating concurrent salaries, and changing budget items, there will be detailed discussions for implementation. As for the four yarn and hemp bureaus, they were originally leased by the Fuyuan Company. The company deliberately stopped work for many days, which greatly affected the lives of all employees. It was specially decided to take them back and take over the operation. Now, 200,000 yuan has been borrowed as funds, and a manager has been appointed to actively prepare, and work will commence within a few days. (July 14)

The Suspect in the Assassination of Xu Is Released on Bail 69

Xiamen Correspondence: The assassination of Xu Zhuoran has become a serious case unprecedented in Fujian. On the one hand, Xu's position in the history of the Party and his relationship with the Min Bureau over the years have made him a key figure in the Min Bureau. His death has attracted great attention from the Fujian Provincial Government and overseas Chinese in Nanyang. On the other hand, after the suspect Chen Delin was arrested, he confessed that he was instigated by Ye Yuan and Chen Yanxiang. Ye has been in charge of the nine schools of Jimei for ten years, and has become the only important figure in the education sector in Fujian Province. Chen Jiageng, the principal of Jimei School, intended to suspend the operation of Jimei School after Ye was imprisoned. Therefore, the movement to support Ye became more urgent. Ye recently wrote a letter to Fang Shengtao in prison, strongly arguing that he was framed. The main points he raised were: (1) If he had a premeditated plan to kill Xu, he would definitely not ask Xu to a certain place, and he would definitely not leave a business card with his name and address in his own handwriting to arouse suspicion. (2) If he had a premeditated plan to kill Xu, he would definitely not write his telephone number. Having a telephone number means that he would be able to contact him by telephone, not ask him to come. (3) He described the course of his grievances and antagonism with Chen Delin, and that he had been arguing with Chen Yanxiang for a long time and was very incompatible with him. Xu was a benefactor to one of them and an old friend to the other. He and Pan Tu Township had asked officials and soldiers to handle the case of theft at the school, and he definitely had no intention of killing Xu to seek grievances and was not close to those close to Xu, etc. Chen Delin's confessions at the Tong'an Education Corps Judicial Office and the Zhangzhou Newly Compiled First Division Military Law Office were all the same, until on July 5, when he was escorted to the Zhangxia Navy Garrison Headquarters Military Law Office for interrogation, Chen suddenly reversed his previous confession and denied that he had participated in the assassination of Xu and that Ye and Chen had instigated the assassination of Xu. That night, Ye Yuan and Chen Yanxiang were granted bail by the court to await trial. According to reports, the headquarters received a telegram from the Civil Service Department of the National Government yesterday, saying, "All parties have telegraphed about this case, and the truth is unclear. Ye Yuan should be temporarily released on bail to await trial, so as not to hinder education." The headquarters immediately notified the court, and the court granted bail. After Ye Yuan was released from prison, Ye Weitai and others, representatives of Jimei School, sued Qin Wangshan, Li Aihuang, Li Hanqing, Zou Chun, and Ye Qingquan, five staff members of Xu's funeral office, to the Siming Court of the headquarters on the 10th, demanding that they be charged with reverse sitting. The headquarters did not accept the case because it belonged to the judiciary.

Qingdao Observatory 70

Groundbreaking Ceremony for the New Equatorial Instrument Dome

Qingdao Correspondence: The groundbreaking ceremony for the new equatorial instrument dome of the Qingdao Observatory was held at 4 p.m. on the 5th of this month at the construction site in the northwest corner of the observatory. Those who attended the meeting included Mayor Ge, Councilors Zhou, Han, and Zhang, the heads of various bureaus, the director of the Agricultural and Forestry Institute, and about 40 other staff members of the observatory. After the ceremony was completed, the mayor performed the groundbreaking ceremony, followed by the director of the observatory reporting the mayor's instructions. The following is an excerpt:

The Director of the Observatory, Jiang, reported on the background of the situation, saying, "Astronomy developed earliest in our country, but the techniques of the ancients are mostly secret and not passed on, and there is no active research on the improvement of observation instruments, so it has fallen behind. This is truly regrettable. In the early years of the Qing Dynasty, Nan Huairen, Tang Ruowang, and others were used to manufacture astronomical instruments for observation, which was quite prosperous for a time. However, since the invention of the telescope, this instrument can only be regarded as an antique. In the early years of the Republic of China, the Central Observatory also planned to build an observatory, but due to the excessive cost, it was difficult to plan, and it was not realized. This observatory was founded by the Germans and managed by the Japanese. The astronomical equipment is also quite simple. After our country took over, because there was a German office in the meteorological observation field, which was badly damaged, it was rebuilt into a dome room, and the original 16 cm diameter equatorial instrument was installed, and a solar and lunar photography device was purchased from the German Zeiss factory for research. By making do with what was available, it could still be used with difficulty. The measured results were also published. In the fifteenth year, the International Meridian Measurement Association invited the observatory to participate in the International Meridian Measurement. Although it was falsely adopted in the international academic community, the astronomical equipment of this observatory has become an urgent matter. At that time, although the former Commercial Port Bureau issued 5,000 yuan for application, it could only purchase high-level instruments and radio transceivers necessary for measuring longitude, etc., and could not provide sufficient equipment. Moreover, the city's financial resources were not enough for this construction, so a plan was formulated to request the Education and Culture Foundation Board of Directors to subsidize 25,000 yuan. In July of the 17th year, the meeting decided to allow the subsidy. Immediately, the prices were investigated in various countries. The price of the French Poilin factory was reasonable, and it was decided to purchase a 32 cm diameter double-tube equatorial instrument of the sky map type, and an 8 cm diameter meridian instrument with a superhuman microscopic ruler for 1,754 pounds of British gold, and 360 pounds of British gold. According to the gold price at that time, there was still a surplus of 1,000 yuan for construction. Since the 18th year, the gold price has been rising daily, and the pre-estimated amount has been insufficient. At that time, another request was made to the association, and an additional 4,000 yuan was obtained, totaling 29,000 yuan of national currency in subsidies from the association. The gentlemen who are enthusiastic about promoting astronomy are very grateful. However, the manufacture of this instrument takes time, so it has not yet arrived. According to a letter from the factory, it can arrive in Qingdao at the end of August. This is the report on the purchase

Page 9

of the instrument. As for the construction, it can be divided into two parts: one is the dome equatorial instrument room, and the other is the meridian instrument room. The diameter of the dome is 7 feet 0.1 meters. It was ordered from abroad, but the value must be more than 1,000 pounds, calculated at the usual gold price, it is still more than 10,000 yuan. It is now made by the Tianjin Shengchang Foreign Firm. It is estimated that the inner iron frame of the dome with a diameter of 7.4 meters is lined with wood, and the outside is wrapped with copper skin with copper rails and a three-horse motor, worth 6,620 yuan of national currency. The observatory has three floors. The first floor is a cellar, storing the motor, and attached with a photography darkroom and enlargement room. The second floor is an office, equipped with a measuring and photographing machine. The third floor is equipped with an equatorial instrument. All engineering instructions have been requested from the Engineering Bureau for review. I would like to thank Yihua Factory for the contract, which costs 4,700 yuan of national currency. The meridian instrument room is built on the west side of the observatory, and the top of the room can be opened and closed. The construction cost is about 800 yuan. It is estimated that the total construction cost is 12,120 yuan. It is estimated that the funds raised are 3,000 yuan allocated by the Commercial Port Bureau for temporary expenses, 2,000 yuan self-raised by the observatory, 2,500 yuan subsidized by the Astronomical Research Institute of the Academia Sinica, and 3,000 yuan recently approved by the mayor. In total, there is still a shortfall of more than 1,600 yuan. However, the entrance to the dome has been requested by the mayor to the Ministry of Finance for tax exemption, but it has not been approved, and several hundred yuan are still required. It is estimated that the shortfall is 2,000 yuan. The observatory is now requesting subsidies from all parties, but it is hoped that the mayor will provide special assistance to complete the work. The above is the report on the construction. At present, the astronomical undertakings in the country are flourishing. The Astronomical Observatory of Guangdong Zhongshan University was established last year. Although the instrument is not very large, the scale is very complete. It is heard that a new observatory is being built and larger instruments are being added. The Nanjing Astronomical Research Institute is also engaged in building an observatory on Zijin Mountain and will be established soon. Other places such as the Peiping Research Institute and Northeast University also have this plan. The construction of this observatory at this time also has considerable reference. Although the instruments purchased cannot be compared with the large astronomical observatories in Europe and the United States, they are not very small. In the future, I hope that the mayor will give instructions and guidance from all the guests."

The mayor's instructions were divided into three points. The first point was the history of Chinese astronomy. Chinese astronomy had considerable inventions in ancient times, but it declined due to the lack of researchers. In the early Qing Dynasty, Westerners Nan Huairen, Tang Ruowang, and others came to China and tried their best to support it, and cast several kinds of bronze instruments. The astronomical undertaking gradually turned around, but since the invention of the telescope, bronze instruments are equal to antiques and are of no practical use. Fortunately, in recent years, a small number of astronomers have purchased and used foreign instruments to vigorously study the astronomical undertaking, and it has begun to emit a glimmer of light. The second point was the evolution of the Qingdao Observatory. The Qingdao Observatory was founded by the Germans and then taken over by the Japanese. It was not taken back by China until the thirteenth year. However, Qingdao's income is limited and cannot support the full development of the astronomical undertaking of the observatory. Fortunately, Director Jiang, like a almsgiver, ran around raising funds, and was finally able to purchase instruments and build an equatorial instrument room, so that there is today's groundbreaking ceremony, and the development of the Chinese astronomical undertaking in the future is also its foundation. The third point was the importance of astronomy. People live in the world, under the sky and on the ground. Astronomy and meteorology are closely related to people's lives. I belong to the military, and first of all, from a military point of view, I have studied all the past wars, and their success or failure is often absolutely related to astronomy and meteorology. The navy is especially important, so the ancients said that the way to be a general must be to know astronomy above and geography below. Other aspects such as food, clothing, housing, and transportation of scholars, farmers, industry, and commerce are closely related to astronomy and meteorology, so all countries are vigorously studying astronomical undertakings, and their progress is rapid. China's astronomical undertaking has already emitted a glimmer of light, and Director Jiang has worked hard to operate it. In the small corner of Qingdao City, there is such a great astronomical equipment, which is really amazing. I hope that everyone will follow Director Jiang and work hard. Their achievements will be considerable, and I have no responsibility to expect. As for the economic aspect, the municipal government will provide assistance within its capacity, etc.

Then, Han An, a city councilor from Qingdao, delivered a speech. Finally, Director Jiang replied, saying that he was flattered by the guidance of the mayor and Councilor Han, and his colleagues will do their best to work hard so as not to live up to the mayor's and Councilor Han's kindness, and thanked the mayor and all the guests. Then, a photo was taken and the meeting adjourned.

Wuhu Quick News 72

Li Fanyi, Director of the Anhui Construction Department, was ordered by the General Headquarters to requisition a dozen buses from the Anhui Provincial Government to be sent to the front to facilitate military transportation. Li obtained seven vehicles from the province and brought them to Wuhu yesterday. He also borrowed six vehicles from the Jing-Wu Road Administration and the Xuan-Wu-Guang Long-Distance Bus Company. Today, he personally sent them to Beijing and reported public affairs to the Central Government. He will also take the newly appointed members of the Provincial Party Affairs Consolidation Committee in Beijing to take the oath and return to Anhui Province to take office.

After Lingshan was captured by bandits for the second time, Xishan, Mabou, Liubo, Zhuang, and other places in the Liuan County area were also harassed. Jinshan 74

An Inhumane Robbery Case: Luo Bugen's family in Kongjiaque West Zhujia Bridge was celebrating the third day of the birth of a son the day before yesterday, and guests came to congratulate them. The house was filled with joy. Unexpectedly, more than 20 bandits came that night, broke into the house, tied up the family, beat them, and forced them to pay money. They also pressed heavy stones on their bodies, injuring a total of four people. Bugen's life was the most dangerous. After being beaten, because he refused to say where the silver was hidden, the bandits used the newborn baby as an exchange condition for forcing silver dollars, claiming that if the hidden silver was not offered, they would kill the newborn baby. Helplessly, Bugen had no cash savings. Although he pleaded repeatedly, the result was that the newborn baby was killed. As for the sugar cakes, gifts, and all items sent by relatives, they were all robbed. A certain female guest's Xiangyun yarn trousers were also stripped off, exposing her lower body. Before leaving, they also borrowed 150 yuan, and agreed to pay the money at the Red Temple near Liujia Weir Village the next day. If they did not comply, they would burn the house in a few days as a threat. They then went to Yang Mingfang's house to rob. Mingfang heard the sound and got up immediately, ran out to beat the gong. The bandits dared to open fire to resist, with no restraint. Therefore, the loss was also huge. Others, such as Jiang Yuzhou's family in Ganxiang West Changyan, the Jin family in the north of Baziqiao, and Zheng Heshang's family in the south of Jiaolian, were all robbed one after another, suffering heavy losses.

Wuxi 76

Attempted Robbery and Kidnapping for Ransom

Wang A-san, from Chenxiang Village, Jingyun Township, Second District, is a farmer with a wife and child. His circumstances are ordinary. Around the spring of this year, he received five or six anonymous threatening letters demanding large sums of money. Wang ignored them and moved his valuables to relatives' homes. However, after 10 PM the other night, more than ten robbers armed with handguns, knives, and clubs knocked on his door, claiming they wanted to rent a cargo barge from A-san. Once inside, the robbers searched everywhere for half an hour, finding nothing of value. Enraged, they planned to kidnap A-san's son, but A-san had hidden himself before the robbers entered. Instead, they kidnapped A-san and took him outside. Not far from his home, a neighbor named Cai A-chuan followed them, pleading for his release. The robbers fired two shots at Cai, who then knelt and begged on A-san's behalf, stating that Wang A-san had no property. After much pleading, the robbers demanded 500 yuan, but Wang A-san agreed to pay 200 yuan. Lacking cash at home, he borrowed from neighbors in the same alley and obtained only 20 yuan. He promised to pay the remaining amount within three days. Before leaving, the robbers left a mast lamp shade, instructing him to meet someone carrying a mast lamp without a shade at Zhangtang Bridge when paying the money. They then released A-san. Unable to pay the remaining amount, A-san reported the incident to the county government yesterday, requesting an investigation.

Lay Down the Butcher Knife and Become a Buddha on the Spot

Xu Xuehai, a resident of Xinglong Bridge East, north gate of the city, is 48 years old and has four sons and three daughters. He hasn't yet taken a daughter-in-law. Xu, along with Jiang Ming-sheng and others, jointly runs the Hongyi Shun butcher shop at the Badou Alley entrance under the North Diaojiao Bridge. The business is doing quite well. However, Xu is usually charitable and enjoys resolving disputes for people, so he has no savings. Recently, due to local unrest, business has been slow. Xu became disheartened with commerce and focused on Buddhism, even muttering to himself and chanting Buddhist mantras, claiming he needed to go to Dushan Mountain in Taihu Lake to become a Buddha. Seeing this, his relatives hired a gasoline boat and a tugboat on the morning of the 14th and, along with his family, sent Xu to Jingxiu in the Tianhou Palace on Dushan Mountain in Taihu Lake, hoping to calm his mind.

Page 10

Hen Lays a Strange Egg

Tang Lan-ying, a female worker at the Yuankang Silk Factory No. 16, Huangbu Mound, outside the north gate of Xiyi, owns a hen that laid a strange egg yesterday afternoon around 3 PM. The eggshell was very soft, and inside was a chicken head. At the rear end of the egg was a worm-like tail, about two inches long, which quickly shrunk to half an inch. The news spread like wildfire, and neighbors flocked to see it, all marveling at the sight. The factory's overseas agent bought it for one yuan to preserve it for physiological research.

New Head of Public Security Bureau Takes Office

Xu Jigui, the newly appointed head of the Public Security Bureau of this county, arrived in Xiyi after being commissioned the day before yesterday. He was originally scheduled to take office on the 15th, but because Director Huang hadn't completed the handover, it was agreed that Xu would take over the bureau at 2 PM on the 16th (today), and a formal inauguration would be held at a later date. Furthermore, Wang Jinbiao, the deputy captain of the bureau's detective team, submitted a request for resignation to Director Huang yesterday due to his wife's illness. At the same time, Inspector Fan Wenshan also submitted a request to Chief Inspector Qian, which was then forwarded to Director Huang, requesting resignation because of urgent matters at home.

Impact of Hurricanes and Rainstorms

Recently, the weather has been unusually hot and muggy. Yesterday morning, the sky suddenly turned cloudy, and heavy rain poured down. Soon after, a hurricane struck suddenly. The old stove in the Li family's house in Caijia Alley outside the north gate collapsed due to disrepair. In Ma Alley, Houqi Street, a section of the wall in a resident's home also collapsed due to the hurricane. A wooden building owned by the Wang family, who own a woodworking shop at Shuigou Head outside the west gate, also collapsed due to the wind. Fortunately, no one was inside, and no one was injured. Many other poorly built houses in the city and countryside were also blown down. Two utility poles between Shitangwan and Fengzhuang were also blown down, disrupting traffic. Around 4 PM, a large poplar tree near Bodu Port was uprooted by the wind, crushing a 12-year-old Jiangbei child named Xiao Sanzi who was passing by under the tree, killing him. At the same time, a large tree in front of the Cao family's house at the end of the sand grave inside Guangfu Gate was also blown down, fortunately without injuring anyone. Because of the continuous rainfall in the fields, the rural crops were not damaged. All the boats, large and small, inside and outside the city, cast anchor to avoid the disaster. Yesterday (15th) morning, starting at 9 AM, heavy rain poured down again, but the wind was slightly less intense than before.

Wujiang 77

Collision of Two Boats Leads to Fatality

Wang Defeng, a native of Jiangbei, made a living by selling mud. A few days ago, he, his wife, his son and daughter-in-law and six others loaded a boat of mud at Jiantian on Luhu Town in Wujiang County to unload goods at Xiadianmiao Kiln in Zhejiang Province. When the boat reached Jiuqu Port, at the junction of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, Sun Songlin, a villager from nearby Yaojiabang, sailed by on a boat harvesting aquatic plants and directly hit the mud boat. An argument ensued, and Sun's long-term worker, Sun Ajin, jumped onto the mud boat and started beating them. Because they were outnumbered, Sun gathered six or seven aquatic weed boats to surround Wang Defeng and his son and daughter. At the same time, he pushed Wang's wife and daughter-in-law into the river. At that time, his second son Wang Guolu was injured and swam to the Luhu Public Security Bureau to report the incident. The bureau immediately sent three police officers to the scene. They saw that Wang and his family of six were seriously injured and arrested Sun Songlin. Unexpectedly, his brother Xianglin dared to twist the patrolman into the field to try to help his brother escape. Fortunately, the police officers fought bravely and arrested the Sun brothers together. Later, a gentleman from the town guaranteed the criminal. The injured party was forced by the power to go to Suzhou for medical treatment. Unfortunately, the injuries were too serious and the bladder bone had been broken. When he returned to Luhu Town, Wang Defeng died at dusk on the 12th. The Public Security Bureau immediately pursued the murderer and first handed over the long-term worker Ajin to the case. The next morning, a secret report was received and Sun Songlin was arrested at the Jingchunlou Teagarden. Immediately, a document was prepared and transferred to the Wujiang County Office for handling. However, his eldest son, Wang Guofu, was in such deep sorrow that his mouth was split and his life was also in danger.

(2) Please send a political police officer from each district to Junfu to assist each district in summoning township chiefs and deputies and urging each township chief and deputy to pursue them from household to household. Jiaxing 82

Villagers in the Northern Countryside Committed Suicide Due to Hunger

The price of rice in Jiaxing is nearly 19 yuan per stone. It is difficult for ordinary people to eat grain, and they are really struggling to survive. The villagers in various villages are mostly empty due to continuous famines. At this time, when the new and old grains are not harvested, it is even more impossible to borrow money. Although the county government has organized low-priced sales, it is still a drop in the bucket and difficult to solve the problem. Recently, it was learned that the Wang family near Meijiadang in the northern countryside had not had rice to cook for days. Someone went out to borrow money to buy rice. When he returned home two days later, his wife had already hanged herself. Out of hatred, he first threw his two children, five and three years old, into the pond, and then hanged himself. The couple of a certain family in Dianshang also committed suicide one after another because they had been without food for many days. In addition, many villagers in various villages are eating chaff and dregs to fill their stomachs and eating only one meal a day. This situation is so tragic that people who hear it feel sad.

The County Government Cautiously Elects Township Chiefs and Deputies

Reasons for the Gradual Increase in Silk Prices

New silk is on the market in the Huasha and Xiafang Bridge areas of Shaoshan. Because silk prices are expensive and silk sales are sluggish in various silk weaving factories, they are all waiting and seeing. Now the harvest of summer cocoons is only about 30%. The silk merchants are preparing raw materials for autumn and winter silk goods, so silk prices are gradually increasing. Since July 10, each silk shop has been selling fine silk for 71 yuan per 100 taels. Because fat silk is combined with summer cocoon silk, it is also priced at 50 yuan, which is two yuan higher than before. It is said that the price will still increase after the beginning of autumn.

Anqing 84

Murder in the Case of Trafficking in Opium from Anhui

Last month, the Anhui Provincial Public Security Bureau cracked down on a large number of opium. Recently, a bloody murder case has occurred as a result. The process is recorded as follows: The opium traffickers outside the Dananmen Gate of Anhui City have been trafficked by Liang Qifeng, Si Lao Er, Ma Lao Wu, Ma Zuoshu and other ten people to Hankou, and the remaining opium merchants are allocated transportation costs. A batch of opium trafficked by Si and others from Hankou a few days ago was unfortunately seized. Another 1,800 taels were spared from being loaded on the ship. The seven traffickers negotiated with Si and others, and Liang Qifeng and others wanted to divide them equally according to the amount of goods purchased by each trafficker. Each 100 taels could be allocated more than 18 taels. Si Liang and others returned to Anhui from Hankou a few days ago and brought back the soil for inspection. Only more than 1,500 taels were found. Liang went to Si on the morning of the 10th to reason with him. He first went to Fugui Building outside Dananmen to use force. After mediation, Liang learned that the city was very close to the south city, and the military police were standing in large numbers, so he invited Si to Yingjianglou Teahouse along the river. Before he could say much, Liang took out a sharp knife about a foot long and stabbed Si's abdomen under the muscles. Blood flowed like a pillar and he fell to the ground in pain. Si's family heard the news and immediately gathered a crowd to support Si back. Liang was also anxious and stabbed his thigh three times with the original knife, mistakenly stabbing his scrotum and lower abdomen, causing serious injuries. He was taken to Boru Hospital in the city and could not be treated and died. Si was also taken to the hospital by his family. Although the injuries were serious, they were not life-threatening. Liang's mother and wife carried Liang's body to Si's house to ask for trouble. Si's family all hid in the hospital. After many mediations, the opium obtained by the opium traffickers was returned at the original price. There were a total of 2,000 yuan, of which 400 yuan was used for Liang's funeral expenses, and the rest was temporarily preserved. If Si was seriously injured and died, it would be divided equally. If Si was fine, Liang's family would get it all to themselves. The bloody case was settled. Educational News

Abolish Middle Schools and Higher Schools

Editing Elementary School Textbooks Should Include the Middle East Massacre 86

The Ministry of Education instructed provincial and municipal education departments to instruct bookstores to pay attention to adding the Middle East Road Massacre when compiling elementary school textbooks to raise awareness. The order reads: "The case approved by the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang No. 9074, the case approved by the Central Secretariat transferred by the Hunan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee submitted by the Xiangxiang County Party Department Executive Committee, 'According to the proposal of the First District Party Department and the First District Branch of the County's Fifth All-County Representative Conference, the truth about the Jinan and Middle East Road massacres should be included in elementary school textbooks so that the people of the whole country can be vigilant.' The conference decided that the National Government should order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs to collect materials and hand them over to the Ministry of Education to compile them into elementary school textbooks and promulgate them throughout the country, and the 70th meeting of the conference also recorded the case and submitted it to the Hunan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee to transfer it to the Central Government for the National Government to order the competent authorities to handle it according to the regulations." In this regard, the Jinan and Middle East Road massacres are the great humiliation of the Chinese National Revolutionary Army since the Northern Expedition. Our country has suffered deeply. The provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee's transfer of the above sections is quite pertinent. Please collect materials on the truth about these two massacres and other national humiliations, and select and consider them to be included in elementary school textbooks to Xue Chi. In addition to informing the Hunan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee by letter and recording the case to the Party Righteousness Curriculum Compilation Committee Primary School Group for reference, the corresponding letter is hereby issued to you to check and handle it and reply. The truth about the Jinan Massacre and other national humiliations in the elementary school textbooks have been compiled separately, and the Middle East Road Massacre should also be added to the editing of elementary school textbooks to raise awareness. The letter was approved and sent to the "province" and "city" to be followed by the bookstores.

Annual Meeting of the Agricultural Society (1) 87

The National Government and the Provincial Government All Sent Representatives to Participate

The Meeting Will Last a Total of Three Days

###

The sixth annual meeting of the New China Agricultural Society was held in Suzhou yesterday. The agenda is divided into three days. The first day's proceedings are recorded below.

History of the Society The organization of the New China Agricultural Society was founded in the 13th year of the Republic of China. The members of the organization are Chinese comrades who studied agriculture in Europe. Western celebrities such as Cai Zimin, Li Shizeng, Wu Zhihui, and French national agricultural college presidents F凡仙, 爱白洛拿, 长冈控瓦君 are all honorary members. It was established in 巴叙阿伯, France, and holds a general meeting once a year to discuss all issues related to agriculture. In the 16th year, most of the members returned to China and formed a society in the capital. This year's annual meeting is the sixth.

Attendees The venue is at Suzhou Agricultural School. More than 40 members from various provinces and representatives from institutions attended. Representatives from the National Government's Ministry of Agriculture and Mines were Pi Zuoqiong, Director of the Jiangsu Government's Agriculture and Mines Department He Yushu, Feng Zigang from the Zhejiang Provincial Government's Design Council, Zhou Weixian from the Zhejiang Construction Department, Mo Dingsen from the Central University Agricultural College, Tan Xihong from the Zhejiang University Agricultural College, and Cai Wuji from the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines' Silkworm Seed Control Institute.

Opening Ceremony The opening ceremony was held at 2:00 PM. Chairman Tan Xihong saluted and then gave the opening speech, reporting on the work done in the past year. The Director of the Jiangsu Agriculture and Mines Department gave a speech, saying that administrative agencies must cooperate with academic agencies, otherwise the progress of both parties will be deformed, and that the regulation of people's food has become a widespread problem. He hoped that the society would conduct more practical research. He Shangping from the European branch reported on the International Agricultural Society and the International Agricultural College welcoming the society to join. Representatives spoke in succession, took photos and adjourned. In the evening, the Suzhou branch and Suzhou Agricultural School held a banquet.

Agenda for Today and Tomorrow The general meeting will discuss the proposal in the morning and afternoon of the second day. Wei will give a speech in the afternoon and have a gathering in the evening. On the third day, they will tour the famous scenic spots in the whole of Suzhou.

Japan Prevents Ideological Excess 88

The More Student Unrest is Suppressed, the More Intense it Becomes

(Central News Agency) Tokyo Correspondence: The training policy for students in Japanese schools takes a strict and oppressive approach, and the prevention of ideas is particularly meticulous. Students have no right to autonomy in school, and alumni associations and student associations are all run by the school. Extra-curricular self-study dormitories and dining halls are also supervised by school personnel, so the life of students has become mechanized. However, extreme pressure breeds rebellion, and prevention is not as good as defense, so that student thinking is gradually becoming left-leaning and secretly contacting left-leaning ideological groups outside the school, and gradually expressing resistance to the school's oppression. The education authorities regard the occasional disturbances in each school as a major problem, so during the era of Minister of Education Katsuda, they advocated ideological guidance and established a student affairs department within the Ministry of Education to specialize in preventing student thinking, and set up an ideological police agency to secretly investigate the actions of students and teachers. Student affairs officers and student affairs officers are set up in each school, guidance officers are adopted for each higher school, special lectures are implemented, and efforts are made to improve student life, promote self-cultivation, and encourage physical education to prevent ideological excesses. The number of tea shops and hemp shops has been increased to facilitate students' comfortable life and wear away their will. However, the practice has been effective, but it has been ineffective. There are a total of 25 national higher schools in the country, which are regarded by the Japanese education community as the most important schools, because their level is equivalent to that of high schools in our country, and they are established for students who aspire to enter the undergraduate program of the Imperial University. The recruitment of students is extremely strict, and most of the students are high-achieving graduates of middle schools, so they are very important. Last year, 11 schools experienced disturbances, accounting for almost half of the total. This year, the Urawa Higher School, the Matsuyama Higher School, and the Third Higher School have successively experienced class boycotts. The education authorities believe that the failure of ideological guidance will seek other ways to prevent it. (7th)

Methods for Disseminating Phonetic Symbols 89

The Ministry of Education formulated 11 methods for teaching phonetic symbols to party and government agencies in Beijing and recently sent a public letter to the party and government agencies in the capital to recommend personnel to participate in the phonetic symbol training meeting and fill in the names of the recommended personnel in the table and send them back in advance. The original text of the methods for teaching phonetic symbols to party and government agencies in Beijing is recorded below.

(1) The Ministry has set up a phonetic symbol training meeting and hired several national language experts as instructors to teach phonetic symbols.

(2) From July 28 to September 28, 19, each class will meet twice a week for two hours each time, for a period of two months.

(3) The Ministry will send letters to the Central Party Department, various ministries, commissions, and offices, the National Government, various academies, ministries, commissions, and other party and government agencies to send staff to the locations designated by the Ministry to learn phonetic symbols. After the learning period expires, they will return to their original agencies to teach and promote them.

(4) The number of people sent by each agency should be based on one person for every 50 existing staff members. Those with less than 50 people will be counted as 50 people.

(5) Those sent for training should be able to speak Mandarin or be similar to Mandarin.

(6) The number of training classes will depend on the number of people sent by each agency, but it is planned not to exceed six classes, with no more than 50 people per class.

(7) The training courses include an overview of phonetic symbols (including the principles of phonetic symbols), the pronunciation method of phonetic symbols, tone exercises, phonetic exercises, and phonetic practice.

(8) Phonetic symbol textbooks will be purchased and distributed by the Ministry free of charge. (9) The tuition fee is four yuan per person, which will be paid by the learning personnel to the original agency at the time of registration (free for Party Department staff).

(10) The training location will be in the classrooms of Central University.

(11) The training time and registration date will be notified temporarily.

The Zhejiang Provincial Local Education Guidance Conference held its opening ceremony yesterday at 8:00 AM at the Provincial Public Education Experimental School. Plan: Lectures will be held to increase academic ability; meetings will be held to understand local conditions and jointly plan progress to seek solutions; an administrative achievement exhibition will be held to compare the implementation in various localities and seek further progress. In the afternoon, a guidance meeting was held. It was reported that as of yesterday, there were over forty proposals from various counties, with the most in the area of elementary education and the second most in the area of social education. The Education Department plans to have a type of local education guidance program, with very detailed specific measures. The conference is scheduled to last fourteen days, with famous people giving lectures every morning and meetings every afternoon. The gathering of elites and the collection of ideas will surely have a significant impact. It has also been decided to hold a local education administrative achievement exhibition for three days. Various counties and cities have already brought their achievement products to the meeting through their representatives. The Education Department has also prepared a large number of achievement products for the exhibition and is currently arranging the display. It is expected that the materials will be rich and will provide valuable research and exploration for education.

Zhejiang Education Department to Establish Correspondence Department for Teacher Training 92

To be Implemented in Three Phases Starting Next School Year

The Zhejiang Education Department, in view of the lack of elementary school teachers in the province and the desire to provide ongoing training for current elementary school teachers, believes that correspondence study is the most appropriate and effective method besides self-study. It is reported that starting from the 19th year (of the Republic), it plans to establish a Zhejiang Provincial Teacher Training Correspondence Department within the Education Department, to be implemented in three phases. After its establishment, its impact and effectiveness will surely be significant. The following are the measures: (1) The purpose of the Teacher Training Correspondence Department is to improve the academic ability of elementary school teachers throughout the province. (2) The Teacher Training Correspondence Department will enroll elementary school teachers from various counties and cities as students. (3) Elementary school teachers in various cities who voluntarily wish to become students should fill out an application form and resume one each before the start of each semester, and can directly register with the Research Department free of charge. However, research books must be provided by the students themselves. (4) The study program for students is divided into three phases, each phase lasting one semester. The books to be studied in each phase are specified as follows (listed separately). However, the Research Department may add, delete, or notify students of any necessary changes to the specified books at any time. (5) Students who complete the first phase will be tested by the Research Department (the method of examination is correspondence or entrusting the local education authorities). Those who pass will continue to study the second phase. Those who pass the second phase examination will study the third phase. Students who complete the three phases and pass the examination administered by the Research Department will be given a certificate. Students who obtain this certificate have the same qualifications as those who have attended vacation workshops three times and are exempt from the oral examination during elementary school teacher registration. However, those who fail the assessment must retake the course. (6) Students should submit a reading report every two months during the study period (report form attached). If there are any questions in the book, they can fill out a form and send it to the Research Department for a reply. However, the Research Department may also raise research questions and ask students to answer them when necessary. (7) The number of students is tentatively set at 1,000. (8) The Research Department is attached to the Zhejiang Provincial Education Department. (9) The head of the Research Department is concurrently the head of the Second Section of the Education Department. (10) These regulations may be amended at any time if there are any omissions.

Zhejiang Education Department Streamlines Teacher Training Institutes in Various Counties 93

Sets and Promulgates Standards for Subjects and Credits

The Zhejiang Education Department, in view of the chaotic content of the teacher training institutes in various counties of the province, has decided to streamline them and has formulated a temporary standard for subjects and credits for teacher training, which has been ordered to be promulgated to various counties. The document states: "Upon investigation, the teacher training institutes in various counties of this province have one-year, two-year, and three-year programs. These types of teacher training institutes are originally of a temporary relief nature. Each county may make appropriate and flexible arrangements based on the needs of the current situation, so there is no need for fixed and uniform methods. In order to streamline the content of the teacher training institutes in various counties, this department has formulated temporary standards for subjects and credits for one-year, two-year, and three-year teacher training institutes based on the actual situation. In addition to separate orders, one copy of the standard is hereby issued and ordered to the county governments to immediately instruct the teacher training institutes in their counties to comply."

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 113

Ticket collector at the theater: "Hey, sir, you're late tonight. The play is already halfway through."

Spectator: "It doesn't matter. Open the door gently for me and let me sneak in quietly. I certainly won't disturb the audience."

Ticket collector: "That's not it. I welcome you to sneak in. I'm just afraid that once the door is opened, everyone will sneak out quietly. That would look terrible on stage."

Judge (to a man accused of stealing a watch): "You have to be more careful in the future. Don't arouse suspicion. You can go now."

Defendant: "Since you're so polite, your honor, then I'll be polite too. I'll just give you this watch as a gift."

Master (rebuking his cook): "Today I came back at dawn. I told you not to tell the mistress. How dare you tell her?"

Cook: "I didn't tell her. It's just that the mistress asked me, 'When did the master come back?' I just replied to her with a very witty remark, saying, 'When the master came back, I was busy making breakfast and didn't have time to look at the clock to see what time it was.'"

Factory supervisor (to a worker): "I just walked in to check on you and saw you just sitting there idly, not working."

A worker: "If you keep sneaking in and out with those rubber-soled shoes, without anyone knowing, then you'll never have the chance to see me working."

The Socialite Murder of Her Husband: The Case of Yan Wenchou 114

The Philippines is imbued with European customs, where education for both men and women is equally developed. Women occupy a considerable position in society, making it arguably the most progressive country in the East regarding women's rights. However, in recent months, a case of a socialite murdering her husband has captured public attention. Each court session is so crowded that there is barely standing room. The next day, newspapers publish the story on their front pages with large headlines. The case has now been tentatively concluded with the verdict from the preliminary court. However, the story is so interesting that it must be shared with readers of "Free Talk."

The plaintiff in this case is a Filipino named Li Nao, a lawyer. He is a promising candidate for governor in a province of the Philippines in the next election. His wife is the younger sister of the president of the Central Women's University, a qualified lawyer and pharmacist, and a teacher at Central University. The couple has been married for over ten years, and their eldest son is fifteen. Unexpectedly, on the night of March 24th this year, Li Nao was murdered at home, sustaining injuries that were not fatal. The prosecutor filed a criminal indictment based on testimonies and evidence from various sources. The reasons given were: (1) The assailant confessed that the wife promised him two hundred dollars as a reward. (2) The driver who transported the assailant saw a woman of similar build to the wife beckoning the assailant into the residence when he got out of the car near the plaintiff's house that night. (3) Detectives found a piece of paper on the staircase in the house where the incident occurred, which read, "He is asleep but not deeply." Handwriting experts in court testified that it was written by the wife. The notebook from which the paper was torn was found in the wife's dressing table. Furthermore, the detective testified that when he found the paper, the wife offered him five hundred dollars to retrieve it. (4) There were two full-length mirrors in the injured man's bedroom, both smeared with chemicals to blur the reflection, clearly to prevent the lawyer from seeing the assailant enter the room in the mirror while lying in bed. The most important evidence was that the main culprit, the driver, confessed to having a love affair with the wife, and that the crime was instigated by her. This improper secret relationship began last July. The plaintiff had once fired the driver, but rehired him at his wife's request, who said their son liked the driver.

Name Anecdotes: Cheng and Qing 115

Hu Shi… Where is he going?

Fang Huan… Just returning.

The explanation of the name of the New Literature scholar Hu Shi is "Where is he going?" in the national language. The meaning of the name of the Old Literature scholar Fang Huan is "Just returning" in the vernacular. I remember one day, a certain politician hosted a banquet to which both Hu and Fang were invited. They both arrived and then left one after the other. During the banquet, a certain issue was being discussed, and they wanted to ask Hu and Fang for their opinions. Someone asked, "Hu Shi, Hu Shi (Where is he going?). Fang Huan, Hu Shi (Where is he going?)." The host replied, "Hu Shi does not know where he is going. Fang Huan is just returning." The guests burst into laughter. Thus, Hu Shi and Fang Huan became a popular anecdote.

The verdict in the case was recently delivered. The judge's verdict was over fifty pages long, not only presenting concrete legal evidence, but also determining from the perspectives of reason and emotion that the wife had committed the act of murdering her husband. (1) The wife hid in the bathroom when she heard her husband calling for help and did not come out to assist. (2) When she saw her husband covered in blood, she did not show any shock or grief, but offered indifferent ridicule, advising her husband to disengage from political affairs. (3) Her son accompanied her husband to the hospital, but she did not go with them. All these circumstances seem unreasonable between a loving couple. It is truly perplexing. If she were not involved in plotting to harm her husband, she would never have shown such indifference to this tragedy. Therefore, the merciless law sentenced the wife to twelve years in prison. The verdict is finalized, and the ironclad case is difficult to overturn.

However, the wife remains very calm. After the verdict was announced, she prepared to appeal to the higher court and told reporters that her conscience was pure and untainted. The lower court may have made a mistake. The higher court has many judges reviewing the case. If there is still justice in the world, she will surely be declared innocent. Her words were so composed, truly befitting a socialite.

As for the plaintiff's attitude towards his wife, he initially stated in court that they were very affectionate and there were no quarrels or animosity. He did not believe that his wife was capable of such cruel actions. However, after the detectives found various pieces of evidence, he agreed to file a public lawsuit. His purpose was also to use the law to silence rumors. Unexpectedly, the case was ultimately established as the crime of murdering her husband. From now on, it is necessary to wait for the verdict of the High Court to determine the outcome. However, that disaster can arise from within the family, and it can be seen that the way of husband and wife is bitter.

Shanghai Returnee Talks About Hongdu: Chen Yuanliang 116

Whenever we read Wang Bo's Preface to the Pavilion of Prince Teng, we cannot help but imagine its prosperity and grandeur in those days. A guest who has recently returned from Hongdu described the recent situation in Nanchang. Here is a record of it for the readers. The rapid advancement of commerce in Jiangxi Province has been troubled by the Communists in recent years. Capitalists in the interior have brought their wealth to the province, resulting in a sudden increase in population and a boom in commerce. Businesses compete to be the most distinctive to attract customers. Glass windows and storefront decorations can be compared to those in Wuhan, especially on Desheng and Zhongshan Roads, which are the busiest. However, rice prices are very high, costing about eighteen yuan per dan (unit of weight). This is because the rice-producing areas of Ganzhou and Ji'an are facing banditry, making transportation difficult and causing a shortage of supply.

The roads are wide and the road administration is extremely meticulous. In addition to the ring road around the city, there are Zhongshan and Desheng Roads. Zhongshan Road is eighty zhang (unit of length) wide and runs from Baihua Islet to the riverside. Desheng Road connects Desheng Gate with Zhongshan Road and is sixty zhang wide. It is currently under construction and not yet completed. Both sides are planted with roadside trees. In the future, when the green leaves provide shade, pedestrians will all be surrounded by greenery.

Transportation is convenient with the Nanchang-Xunyang Railway, which takes only four hours by express train to reach Nanchang. There are public buses on the Nanchang-Zhangshu section. By waterway, it goes east through Hekou and Guangxin to Zhejiang, and south through Ganzhou to Fujian.

The newspaper situation is also very developed. There are the Republic Daily, Nanchang News, Industrial and Commercial News, and Commercial News.

Impressions of a Trip to the East (8) Qian Hua 117

The reporter stayed in Osaka for less than a day before hurrying to Tokyo. Zeng Junyanhua rushed back to Kobe to handle welcoming the Chinese athletes to the East. He was unable to see the sights of Osaka. He only visited the Osaka Asahi Shimbun. Later, although he intended to revisit after the Far Eastern Games, he was ultimately unable to fulfill his wish. He still feels regret to this day. Fortunately, he met Mr. Ruan Weicun, a reporter for our newspaper stationed in Osaka, who described the situation in Osaka in great detail. He was even clearer about the current situation of the overseas Chinese. Most of what is described in this article is from Mr. Ruan. Osaka has a long history. It was first called Daeho. During the reign of Emperor Ojin (about two thousand years ago), it was renamed Takatsu and a castle was built. In the early Meiji era, Takatsu was renamed Osaka Prefecture. Later, a city was established. After the Meiji Restoration, the port was opened. Osaka Prefecture is divided into three cities: Osaka City, Amagasaki City, and Sakai City. Osaka City is further divided into thirteen wards, each with a city office. Osaka Prefecture has a circumference of about two hundred and forty Chinese miles. Osaka's industry and commerce occupy a very important position in the world. Six or seven out of ten Japanese goods seen in the world market are produced in Osaka. The main exports are cotton yarn and cotton cloth, with an annual export value of about four or five hundred million Japanese yen. Osaka has three commodity exchanges, which are the source of cotton yarn and cotton prices in East Asia. In addition, there are various factories, including five shipyards, all of which can build giant ships of 10,000 tons or more. There are many spinning mills, the largest of which is Kanebo. There are more than two hundred banks with capital of several million yen. In terms of shipping, Osaka is the center of the Osaka Shosen Kaisha. The initial capital was only 100 million yuan, which was founded in the same year as our China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. However, due to the development of business over the years, its current strength is ten times greater than that of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. There are a total of 180 giant ships with a total deadweight of more than 400,000 tons. The shipping routes cover the globe. The most famous attractions in Osaka are Tennoji Temple, Takarazuka, Minoo, Hamadera, Obhama, and Sumiyoshi Park. Another thing that is worth paying attention to is that there is a very large arsenal in Osaka Prefecture. It was founded in the early Meiji era and greatly expanded after the Russo-Japanese War. There are now more than 20,000 workers manufacturing the latest products, which can compete with major factories around the world. To this day, they are still working day and night. Inside Osaka Castle, ammunition depots are everywhere. The richness of the storage can be imagined. The Japanese plan is far-reaching and the intention is deep, which is enough to get a glimpse of it. In terms of military preparations, the 4th Division of the Army is stationed in Osaka, plus a regiment of military police. This is the peacetime military strength. In the event of an emergency, a total of 200,000 people can be mobilized, including 150,000 Osaka reservists (i.e., retired conscripts) and youth groups.

The Republic Daily is run by the Party Headquarters and has the widest circulation. The evening paper is the Jiangxi Evening News, which appears after 5 p.m.

The entertainment for the masses includes the Xinxing Stage, located in Zhonggulou. Men and women perform together. In addition to traditional operas, they also perform Shanghai-style serial new plays to attract audiences. The lowest price is twenty cents. There are two cinemas, Lequn and Jiangxi, which both screen domestic films. There is also the Xiansheng Amusement Park, which opened on the fourth of last month. The building has four floors, with various performances from the north and south. It is like the Great World and New World in Shanghai. In addition to the entrance fee, tourists must also pay ten copper coins for education. The enthusiasm of the people of Jiangxi for education is evident.

The construction of parks: Baihua Islet lacks the charm of Shaolin Gully, only decorated with artificial hills. Usually, light boats meander in the islet, but in the summer the water dries up. It has now been rebuilt as Zhongshan Park, carefully managed, and manufactured artificially. Even in the long summer, it makes green water into channels to rival the West Lake.

The charming road names: In addition to Baihua Islet, the fragrant and pleasing road names include Cuihua Street and Qiaobu Street. Cuihua Street has many jewelry stores, and Qiaobu Street has many summer cloth shops.

The division of prostitutes: Prostitutes are divided into two factions, the local gang and the Yangzhou gang. Most of them gather in the Yangjiangjun Alley area. They have cut hair and wear boots, dressed fashionably. Official prostitutes are mostly found in Wutongshu and other places. Locals call them MISS, but I don't know what it means. The decay of historical sites: The Pavilion of Prince Teng was completely destroyed by fire due to lack of fire prevention. Although it was rebuilt on the original site, it was done hastily and failed to reach even one ten-thousandth of its former glory. It is now occupied by the Water Police Bureau, refusing tourists. The flying pavilions and flowing vermilion of that year have all turned to ashes. Lingering over the scenic spots, one cannot help but sigh.

Eastern Travel Correspondence (12) Wu Xiaohou 118

(Unfinished) Tokyo's Water and Sewer Facilities: Water is an essential element for human life, and is very important for residents' drinking water, municipal fire prevention, and rural operations. Japan is an island nation surrounded by water. The construction and management of water and sewer facilities has been ongoing for over three hundred years without stopping. As of the end of December of Showa 3, the number of water supply households in the city has reached 338,769, and the water supply population has reached 2,070,505 people. The average total water supply per year has reached 138,118,191 cubic meters.

(1) Water Supply Facilities: The origins of the water supply facilities began with the diversion of the clear spring of Inokashira outside the city by Okubo Shusui, a vassal of Tokugawa Ieyasu. It was gradually improved by Ietsuna, the fourth shogun, and Qingyouwei, and gradually became complete. Currently, the water source for the water supply is the Tama River basin. Regarding the development near the water source, water quality deterioration, and prevention of unclean objects, several facilities such as the Mikawashima Sewage Treatment Plant and the Garbage Disposal Plant have been established. There are also detailed equipment for testing drinking water, preventing epidemics, and extinguishing fires. Such as the adjustment of reservoirs, the construction of all water channels into culverts and tunnels to prevent evaporation or leakage, and the distribution of water pumps in the city. Everything is well organized and orderly. Currently, the average daily water supply in the city is 377,372 cubic meters. The maximum daily water supply is 459,160 cubic meters. The minimum daily water supply is 279,411 cubic meters. The average water supply per person per day is approximately 186 cubic feet. The cost of facilities up to the first year of Showa was more than 35.5 million yuan. The rapid construction work after the reconstruction cost 5.13 million yuan. According to the complete water supply expansion plan set thereafter, the total budget required is approximately 67 million yuan.

(2) Sewer Facilities: Sewer facilities are extremely important for public health and hygiene, and they are most closely related to the facilities of the water supply. Since the basic sewer improvement design in the 41st year of Meiji, the first phase of construction began in the Asakusa area of Shitaya Ward in the 44th year of Meiji. In the 5th year of Taisho, due to the disaster of rainwater flooding, the second phase of construction was extended to Kyobashi, Nihonbashi, Marukomachi, and Shiba Ward in the 9th year of Taisho, in the central area of the city. The third phase of construction was the radical advancement of reconstruction after the Great Earthquake. The sewer facilities of the entire city began to be brilliantly prepared. According to statistics, the sewer system in Tokyo is divided into three areas. (1) Shiba Ward, Asabu, Akasaka, Marukomachi, Yotsuya, Ushigome, Koishikawa, Nihonbashi, the eight wards, as well as most of Hongo, Kanda, and Kyobashi, and part of Shitaya. (2) All of Asakusa Ward, most of Shitaya, Kanda, and Hongo. (3) All of Honjo, Fukagawa, and other wards, and Tsukishima in Kyobashi. The above-mentioned three areas of the sewer system each have an area, and each has a pump station and a disposal plant. After the reporter finished visiting the sewer facilities in various places that day, it was still early. I remembered that my Japanese friend, Mr. Miyazaki Ryusuke (leader of the Japanese Social Democratic Party), had come to China in the summer of the year of Jiji to participate in the memorial ceremony for Mr. Sun Yat-sen. He lived in Takadanobaba outside Tokyo, which can be reached directly by tram. Therefore, I went to visit him with Mr. Uchida Takeo and Ms. Du Huairong. He and Mrs. Byakuren came out to meet us and received us warmly. He also presented us with a calligraphy with the inscription "Popular Autonomy" and a recent photo. He also wrote "The First River of People's Governance." Ms. Huairong also wrote "Sino-Japanese Friendship" to present to Mrs. Byakuren. In a reunion in a foreign land, the feelings of old friends are strong. Later, Miyazaki sent a half-length photograph as a reward by post. He also gave two quatrains. The thick gift is given to both beauties. The gracefulness is clear and beautiful. Bringing it back is like a thousand gold treasures. This is something that cannot be done without affection. I want to comfort Mr. Kekaso. I will send a small photo in the mail. I know that the shape is ugly and ashamed to exchange it. Stay for him and wait for the snow swan.

The Cotton Yarn Market is Weakened by Overseas News

The yarn market is slightly weak, and the situation is softening, mainly because the overseas cotton yarn market is uniformly trending downward. The sales of existing yarn are also sluggish, and all gangs [帮, merchant groups] lack a sense of excitement, so most people are bearish. However, the factories are still unwilling to relax, and there are many who are turning to scalping. But judging from the general trend, it is difficult to rise sharply, and it is not easy to fall sharply for the time being. Therefore, the current situation is still a spiral one.

Due to Rain, the Rice Market is Extremely Depressed

Yesterday, due to rain, no ships arrived in Zhabei, and transactions in this street were also suspended due to rain. Although there was a price discussion at noon at Bian Yuan River, there was no trading because it was difficult to open the measuring container. The large stocks were still around 19.5 yuan. Northern japonica rice in these one or two markets will be at rock bottom. The Huangdu cargo ships, which have been abandoned for a long time, will soon be opened and sold in Shanghai because they are useless to hold onto. However, the dispute between the Rice Merchants Association and the Rice Shops Association, as well as the shortage of rising and falling goods, was discussed in an important meeting last night, but there was no solution. The Rice Merchants Association decided that it would be difficult to pay in advance for the goods after the assessment of the measuring container, so there are still difficulties in assessing the rising and falling prices of japonica and indica rice in the future. The whole day's situation here was extremely lonely. There is no source of Baijing at the river under the South of Shanghai, and the Sutong goods are gradually becoming bland, still priced at 21 yuan. This kind of market is like a stereotyped article, and the yin and yang changes are still not developing. The association's transactions are extremely small, almost resembling a standstill. Although the warehouses lack storage, the atmosphere in the market is not panicked. Moreover, this port still has more than 30,000 stones of stockpiled japonica rice, and the authorities have completed the registration. Of course, the necessary sanctions will be adopted, so although no goods have arrived from the north and south recently, the large stocks are instead showing sluggishness.

Another Message of Optimism About Rice Prices 127

This year, the harvest in the Liyang area is very good, and the early sharp rice will be available next month. In the past two days, Xixin reported that Liyang rice merchants had already been trying to sell rice in Xixin, and the quoted price was 4.5 yuan. This kind of market price is about 13.5 yuan in Shanghai, and the number of tons sold is irrelevant. It is currently being negotiated, so the future of the rice market is not pessimistic. In addition, the early rice harvest in the Wuhu area is also abundant, and according to news from that place, the new rice will be available soon. Therefore, foreign rice in Wuhu has recently been transferred to neighboring counties, so the price of foreign rice may have to decline after the stagnation in the consumption in Jiangxi Province.
