Diesel Engines for Automobiles by Paige-Graham 183

Highly Effective and Very Economical

Last year, one of the great advances in the automatic machinery industry was the adoption of the Diesel internal compression engine on automobiles and airplanes. The Diesel engine used on automobiles has not yet left the trial period, but it has been very successful in airplanes, especially for the efficiency it produces when burning low-grade fuel. The first Diesel engine was invented by German Rudolf Diesel in 1897. It was crude and heavy and not suitable for practical use. Later, it was gradually improved, and the machine body and weight were both modified until it was adopted by steamships. Its economy is beyond the reach of other engines. It is even more suitable for large ships at sea. Before 1919, Diesel engines were not noticed by Americans, but in that year, they were praised by various machinists and recognized their strength. Oil mining and transportation of oil in the west, from oil wells to refineries, in large cities and their surroundings, must use a power machine to generate great power, and the cost must be saved.

The weight of the power machines used in oil mining areas is not affected. Therefore, Diesel engines are used everywhere in oil fields. Today, in oil-producing areas, all kinds of stationary Diesel engines can be seen everywhere. They are stable when used and have great results. This kind of engine can be used for a long time. It can handle fast or slow speeds, day or night. Since 1919, the towing, transportation, and fishing industries have flourished along the Atlantic and Pacific coasts and in seaports around the world. As a result, Diesel engines have also been widely used. Therefore, automatic mechanical engineers know that the adoption of this engine in automobiles and airplanes is not far away and will be greater than any other use. But using an engine weighing 1,100 pounds in an automobile is something that ordinary people cannot imagine. Who would believe that it could be driven at 50 miles per hour? As for having 23 million steamships equipped with this engine and sailing at sea, wouldn't that be a joke? Therefore, before 1919, automatic mechanical engineers viewed Diesel engines very indifferently.

Dr. Sperry's first Diesel engine invented in the United States weighed 22 pounds per horsepower. There is no doubt about its great efficiency, but it is far from being used in automatic locomotives. Last year, Dr. Shi also built a Diesel engine, reducing the weight to three pounds per horsepower. In addition, one weighing one and a half pounds is also being tested. Automatic mechanical engineers regard this latest style and its theory as practical and valuable.

Dr. Tauber, one of the giants of Diesel engine research in the United States, built a machine with compression as its main purpose, weighing two and a half pounds per horsepower. Currently, there are forty companies in the United States testing this Diesel engine for automobile use. A few months ago, German inventor Brockmann was granted a patent for the electrolytic gas production method for Diesel engine fuel injection. The main purpose of this method is to alleviate the tightening force on the walls of the cylinder when it is compressed. Its value is better understood in Europe than in America, because Europe is often a huge testing ground for automatic mechanical objects.

Speaking of the basic use of the Diesel engine, it is very simple. Inject fuel oil into the cylinder and draw in air. The air is compressed and heated, and as a result, the oil burns on its own. To achieve maximum efficiency, it is necessary for the walls of the cylinder to have a huge tightening force. Therefore, it is very obvious that the metal required to manufacture this machine must have extremely high resistance. However, on the one hand, it cannot be too heavy, otherwise the economic efficiency of operation will be suppressed by the capacity. In recent years, manufacturers of Diesel engines have used cast iron as the material. Recently, a kind of lead mixture was invented in the automotive industry, which has great strength and is also light. Automotive machinists have now used lead to make Diesel engines, and it is said that the results are very good. As for airplanes, there is no problem. In a few years, lead will be used entirely.

If the Diesel engine is used in automobiles instead of the current gasoline engine, the cost will only be one-fifth of that. There is no need to use spark plugs. Management is smooth and simple. All dangers of incomplete combustion and adjustment can be avoided, because each cylinder is automatically installed and adjusted. A few years ago, a fuel using dicarbonyl gasoline was invented, using the kinetic energy of each piston in the cylinder. This fuel is more expensive than ordinary gasoline. Although it is very effective, it is not popular with drivers. If a Diesel engine is used, the result is the same, and the cost is still lower than that of ordinary gasoline.

The cylinder of the Diesel engine can be cleaned after each action, because the force of the compressed air is very effective. Lower-grade fuel can be used. The machine must be made of metal to maintain the tightening force. This is a problem studied by automotive machinists around the world. Recently, the price of automobiles has become lower and lower, and the use of airplanes has become more and more widespread. Automatic mechanical engineers are seeking economical and effective power in order to have a large output. The use of Diesel engines has been very widespread in recent years, and it is no longer the same as when Rudolf Diesel invented the machine in 1897.

Mack Motor Engineers and Workers Experienced in Manufacturing Eight-Cylinder Cars 184

The excellent performance of Mack eight-cylinder cars is rare in the world. The root cause is that the machinists and workers have mechanical knowledge and experience. Therefore, the manufacturing is meticulous and the work is serious. Mack's various eight-cylinder car products are extremely exquisite and universally praised.

In the past four years, the personnel of the Mack factory have been focusing on large eight-cylinder cars, working together to research and improve them, with great results. Since 1926, they have changed their policy, abandoning the old and replacing it with the new. Now, in addition to manufacturing large eight-cylinder cars, there are no other types. The work of the entire factory personnel is focused and not distracted. Mack machinists and workers can be said to be experts in manufacturing large eight-cylinder cars.

The minds of the people in the Mack Machinery Department have all been "eight-cylindered." The first manufacturing was not done blindly, but was prepared early and tested in advance. Therefore, in these four years, although the time was very short, the results were quite impressive. The greatest goal now is to make the large eight-cylinder car a car with excellent operation and economical durability.

Now, all employees of the Mack factory, from workers to department heads, are all focused on the design and construction of large eight-cylinder cars. In the past, eight-cylinder cars were considered difficult, but now they are not. The manufacturing method and organization of eight-cylinder cars are regarded as normal and without any difficulty.

Mack cars have many features, such as tuners, dual low-drop exhaust pipes, etc. When workers manufacture and assemble them, they not only know the object but also understand the reason. This kind of knowledge and scholarship cannot be obtained in a day or two. It is only after four years of work experience that today's success has been achieved.

Mack managers and salespersons all know the advantages of large eight-cylinder cars. The style is exquisite, and the operation is quick. Even car owners and customers are aware that eight-cylinder cars are becoming increasingly popular and are paying close attention. Among eight-cylinder cars, Mack can be said to be the best. It is truly worthy of being the leader of eight-cylinder cars. To learn more about eight-cylinder cars, you can inquire at the Mack Motor Manufacturing Factory. They will definitely provide a satisfactory answer.

The first Mack large eight-cylinder car was initially completed in 1926. In the past four years, various eight-cylinder cars, the No. 79 eight-cylinder car, the No. 69 eight-cylinder car, and the Mack-Luxford car have been sold at reasonable prices, ranging from US$1,000 to US$2,300. The goods are genuine, the price is fair, and they are cheap and beautiful.

Statistics on Car Accidents in Shanghai in the First Half of the Year 185

A Total of 5,381 Incidents

Exceeding the Records of Previous Years

Cars are like tigers in the city. Even a child of three feet knows that they can kill people and cause disasters. Shanghai is the largest commercial port in Asia. Since the automobile industry has flourished, the number of vehicles in the city also tops other cities in the Far East. When there are many vehicles, it is easy to cause accidents. This is inevitable. We only need to read the newspaper to see that car accidents injuring people happen almost every day. According to the statistics of the Shanghai Municipal Council, the number of car accidents injuring people in the Concession in the first half of this year has exceeded the statistics of previous years, creating a new record that has never been seen before. The number of people injured is as high as several hundred, and the financial losses are even more inestimable. The authorities should strive to remedy this bad phenomenon. Therefore, the Municipal Council has repeatedly urged

Page 24

pedestrians to pay attention, and on the one hand, also repeatedly warned drivers, in order to reduce the number of accidents.

From January 1st to June 30th, in the six months before and after, there were a total of 5,381 car accidents in the Shanghai Public Concession. Among them, 63 people were injured and died, and 1,967 people were injured but did not die. However, among these 1,967 people, there are also many people whose injuries cannot be restored and will be disabled for life. Therefore, the financial losses are really uncountable. In June, nine people were crushed to death by cars, including six pedestrians. When they were walking, they were not careful and wanted to cross the road, so they were hit by cars. Comparing all the car accidents in the first half of this year with last year, there were only 4,642 in the first half of 1929. The difference is obvious.

In 1929, there were a total of 9,691 car accidents. Based on the situation in the first half of this year, if the methods adopted by the Municipal Council in the second half of the year to eliminate accidents are ineffective, then the number of accidents this year will exceed previous years by a large margin. This can be asserted. In June of this year, there were 939 accidents, in which 349 people were injured. The report for March was 982, which is even more than in June. Among all the accidents in June, there were 132 bicycle accidents, of which 70 were caused by the carelessness of the rider. There were 710 car accidents, and the number of people injured was 212. There were 50 people injured by bicycles. There were 16 people injured in streetcar accidents, and there were also 100 public bus accidents, in which 70 people were injured. In addition, other means of transportation, including rickshaws, injured 58 people in total.

According to the investigation reports of the patrolmen on the accidents that occurred in various places, in June, 153 people were injured in all cases because they were careless and hit by cars. Nanjing Road is a place where cars and horses are concentrated. The number of accidents in June still accounted for the majority. Two people died immediately after being hit. The second was Sichuan Road, where one person was crushed to death. One person died near Xinzha Bridge, two people on Zhejiang Road, and one person on Yangshupu Road. During this summer, there are more cars on the road in the evening than usual, because they are all out for a drive. Moreover, Chinese people are accustomed to having too many passengers in a car, and these vehicles are mostly rented from car dealerships. The drivers are not very experienced, and they drive on the road at speeds that exceed the limit and honk their horns frequently, causing other vehicles and drivers to be confused. As a result, accidents are more likely to occur. The patrolmen are now paying attention to these drivers. On the one hand, they are also urging pedestrians to be vigilant when walking, so that they can avoid disasters. Overtaking a car on a narrow road is also prohibited. The speed should not be too fast. When driving, everyone must drive on one side and not be chaotic, in order to avoid accidents and not injure a person or a thing.

Diesel Cars by Ding Zuce 186

The fuel for modern cars is generally gasoline, so they are often called gasoline cars. Gasoline is a relatively expensive commodity among fuel oils. Although users of automobiles in producing countries or non-producing areas can still get an economical means of transportation, the production of gasoline will gradually decrease, and the desire to seek a new, more economical fuel is what the industrial and commercial sectors think about every day. A few years ago, some people advocated using alcohol and diesel as substitutes for gasoline. The experiment of alcohol has achieved considerable results, but its value has not been seen to be very cheap. As for diesel, it is indeed the cheapest of liquid fuels, and it has been adopted as fuel for land-based stationary engines and ship engines, and it has shown very suitable and economical results. The reason why it cannot be used as fuel for automobile engines is that the engine body is too heavy and the operation is not sensitive. Now the German Mercedes-Benz (MERCEDES-BEOZ) car factory has broken through the above-mentioned difficult problems and created diesel passenger cars and freight cars, while in the United States, which manufactures the most cars in the specialized field, there has been no official product heard. This is because the United States has cheap gasoline supply.

Recently, the American Cummins Diesel Engine Company installed a ship diesel engine manufactured by them on a 1925 model car chassis to test whether the diesel engine can replace the gasoline engine and to see what the differences are. After the car was fully assembled, it started from Columbus, passed through Indiana, Detroit, and arrived in New York. It returned from New York to its original departure point, with extremely satisfactory results.

This test drive totaled 2,780 miles, passing through all kinds of roads, including plains and mountains. The maximum speed reached 55 miles per hour. The stability of the journey was almost the same as that of a gasoline car. Diesel is only sold for eight cents to one dime a gallon in the United States. (Approximately 25 to 30 cents in Chinese currency.) It greatly surprised the engineering community.

The diesel engine used this time was a four-cylinder type. The cylinder inner diameter was four and a half inches. The stroke was six inches. The horsepower was 50 horsepower. The car used was not specially manufactured. It was an old-style car (1925 model), which had its original gasoline engine removed, and a ship diesel engine was cut off its heavy legs and put in. The other parts of the car were not changed.

The diesel car was driven by Mr. Cummins, the manager of Cummins Diesel Engine Company. Its driving stability was no different from that of ordinary cars. When driving in the most prosperous areas of New York from 4 pm to 5 pm, there was no difficulty encountered. It was not noticed by pedestrians either. The exterior of the car had no special shape and no special sound. Except for the small words "Cummins Company Diesel Test Car" written on the tire cover hanging behind the car, there were no other marks.

Before this test, the company had no preparations. On the day of departure, the car was processed for only one hour and five minutes from 9:30 in the morning before it was put on the road. Until the end of the trip, it traveled a total of 25 hours, 2,780 miles, and used 102 gallons of diesel. At seven cents of US dollars per gallon, it cost a total of more than seven US dollars for fuel. Based on the same type of gasoline car, it would cost 86 US dollars for gasoline to travel the same distance. This proves the simplicity of diesel cars. The consumption is only one-twelfth of that of gasoline cars, and the weight of the car is 6,000 pounds, about twice as heavy as a gasoline car.

According to Mr. Cummins, he claimed to people that he only wanted to prove this time that ship or ordinary mobile diesel engines

can also be used in cars. He had heard people talking about the clumsiness of diesel engines and that it was not suitable to drive cars with them. He personally tested it to prove the untrustworthiness of rumors. He also believes that the success of the first test is most suitable for diesel engines to be installed on heavy vehicles such as freight cars, agricultural vehicles, or public buses. It is also possible to install them on ordinary passenger cars.

Overseas Car News 187

This year, the automotive industry will undergo significant changes. American statistics expert Mr. Barresgo recently discussed "The Automobile Industry in 1930" at a meeting of the Western University Club in New York. He stated that this year, the American automobile industry will experience drastic changes. The reason is that smaller companies will inevitably be acquired by two or three major corporations. Mr. Barresgo believes that, according to statistics, the output of the two major companies accounts for 65% of the total, and this 65% also accounts for 80% of all low-priced cars. In such a situation, smaller companies will find it extremely difficult to compete with large corporations with strong capital. As a result, they will inevitably be acquired. If you don't believe it, observe in three or four years; America will only have three or four major companies left at that time, and their products will represent the entire United States. Furthermore, banks have repeatedly indicated in recent years that financial health is not as robust as in the past. Therefore, this year's trend will be that the sales of low-priced cars will be more robust than those of high-priced cars. Large corporations, with sufficient capital, have extremely low unit costs, making it easy to win the favor of the public. Smaller companies, lacking the ability, reluctantly lower their prices. However, if large corporations make things difficult for them by deliberately lowering car prices, smaller companies will suffer significant losses, and their operations will be difficult to sustain. This phenomenon is becoming increasingly apparent, and the actual situation is undeniable. Currently, car sales can reach 3,500,000 units, and it is difficult to expect any higher figures. His words contain considerable truth.

At this time, because the government does not allow it, they have invented another type of device that only allows calls when the car is stopped and becomes ineffective when the car is moving. In this way, passengers will not talk loudly in the car, and when the vehicle is damaged, they can call for help. Such a compromise solution can satisfy both parties. Recently, this device has been submitted to the government for testing. It is unknown what the officials in charge think of it.

Choosing Good Gasoline is the Only Way to Save Money (Continued) 188

KH

Why Does the Engine Knock?

In other words, about 25% of the heat is converted into work, and the rest is dissipated into the air through the cooling water and the exhaust pipe.

Even if the wisdom of engineers can restrain some waste, the expansion is inevitably limited. Because the compression of the mixture before ignition has a certain limit, and because the upward stroke and downward stroke of the engine are equal, the expansion is limited by the compression that we can implement. After the mixture is ignited, we want it to expand powerfully on the one hand, and we want it to expand evenly on the other hand. If the expansion is too powerful, the engine will move violently and unstably, which will inevitably cause knocking and vibration, lose original power, be over-burnt, and the car will perform poorly on mountains. Worse, if this condition persists, spark plugs and valves will be damaged, as will bearings. As a result, car repair shops can make a fortune from it.

Therefore, preventing knocking is an essential element of modern good gasoline. I will not talk about the words of experts. I can say that the creation of this characteristic is achieved by examining the combustion speed of the mixture in the cylinder, selecting the most suitable raw materials to restrain the combustion speed, and then processing and mixing it, so that the resulting gasoline contains extremely high anti-knock properties and can withstand the most severe compression.

The Characteristics of Driving 189

The second element of gasoline, of course, is the convenience of driving, which is known to everyone. Because the most annoying thing is that the car is sluggish and difficult to drive. A car that is sluggish and does not drive is harmful to the battery, harmful to people's temperament, and, what is more, harmful to the engine. Because if starting fails repeatedly, excessive raw gasoline is sucked into the cylinder, washing away the protective lubricant on the cylinder wall, eventually damaging the engine. All major gasoline companies pay great attention to the characteristics of driving. It is now well known that the specific gravity and weight of gasoline have nothing to do with its volatility and ease of starting. What needs to be paid attention to is its mixture.

Although I have been involved in the automotive industry for many years and pay close attention to all its aspects, large and small, I never knew that gasoline production had become such a specialized science. Mechanical Monsters 192

With this engine, equipped with various instruments sufficient to verify its operation, major gasoline companies test various types of gasoline. Not only can they determine its anti-knock properties, but they can also determine its power efficiency and its characteristics. The companies formulate standards on the one hand and seek progress on the other, deliberately overthrowing them.

The next day, another method is used to turn this room into a tropical climate. The small Morris moves freely and happily in this extremely cold and extremely hot environment.

I often like to use a specific brand of gasoline. According to my recent experience, this is actually necessary today. I would like to introduce this method to readers. (End)

Hankou City Street Tree Planting Plan Wu Fei 193

Hankou city, in terms of its terrain, is not very suitable for afforestation. However, places such as city streets and lake embankment sides are all suitable for planting trees to enhance the scenery. As for maintaining public health and utilizing the main and auxiliary products of trees, they are secondary. Now I will talk about the street tree planting in the afforestation plan, summarizing its main points, roughly divided into three aspects, namely, one is the arrangement of existing roadside trees, two is the new planting and replanting of roadside trees this year, and three is the planting plan for roadside trees in the future.

There is also the arrangement of existing roadside trees. The roadside trees in Hankou City started in concessions and special zones. Later, the Chinese界 also followed suit in planting. However, the street police protection is weak, and they are often destroyed. The withered, dead, and aging trees are sparse and uneven. Moreover, the tree species and sizes planted before and after the same street are different and uneven, so they are unsightly. Now the municipal government has prepared four matters that should be arranged to remedy it. (1) All withered, dead, and aging existing roadside trees should be removed, and replanted with trees of the same species and size as the existing trees. (2) For those planted too densely, carefully sparse them to gradually make the plant spacing consistent. The dug-up trees should be replanted in other places. (3) When two or more different types of trees are mixed on the same street, remove the one that grows worse and replace it with a tree of the same species and size as the one that grows better. If there are trees of older age on the same street, use the pruning method to control the growth of the older ones, so that their shape and size gradually approach the youngest trees. All these four are plans for the arrangement of existing roadside trees.

Planting roadside trees this year In order to enhance the beauty of the city and maintain hygiene, roadside trees are specially planted on the newly built Yanjiang Road and Zhongzheng Road. The tree species used on Yanjiang Road are French plane trees, thorn cypresses, and palm trees. Zhongzheng Road uses large-leaf willows. The roadside trees that have been planted on each street have suffered repeated external damage, and many have withered. It is also planned to replant them all to enhance the appearance. The tree species selected should be of the same species and size as the existing trees on each street. The tree species are trees such as plane trees, locusts, catalpa, ash trees, golden rain trees, poplar trees, and large-leaf willows, which are used for roadside trees, and it is advisable to use those with a tree height of more than one zhang, a chest height diameter of more than one inch, lush branches and leaves, and a straight trunk. The newly planted trees: (1) On Yanjiang Road, a tree planting zone with a width of one meter is set up on the sidewalk. The row spacing is about four and a half meters from the houses. Other roadside trees are planted in the lawn, one meter away from the road, and one plant is planted every eight meters. About 124 plants are needed for both sides. However, no planting is done at the intersections of streets and alleys. (2) On Zhongzheng Road, one tree is planted every seven meters, and about 300 plants are needed for both sides. The sidewalks on this road are very narrow and not enough for planting. It is planned to dig holes on both sides of the road, about 0.75 meters from the human-shaped ditch. At the intersection of the streets, planting should start at six or seven meters from the intersection. The number of trees to be replanted on each street is a total of 1,564 plants. The plant spacing and the distance from houses for replanted trees should be in accordance with the original distance of the planted trees to show uniformity. The roadside trees on each street that are planted too densely should be carefully dug up and replanted in other places. On Fu Dong Road, because the side line is too narrow, it is inconvenient to set up supports. It is now decided to widen the side line by one meter on each side to avoid hindering the growth of the trees and to facilitate the setting up of

Page 26

Set up supports. Therefore, the seedling fee, excavation fee, packaging fee, transportation fee, planting fee, support setting fee, and miscellaneous fee for the new posts or sleeve plantings to be carried out this year total 2,550.874 yuan.

Future tree planting plan The tree planting of roadside trees must have the following four conditions: (1) The shape and color of the trees should be able to exert natural beauty and enhance the beauty of the city streets. (2) There should be shade to shield the summer sun without hindering the dryness of the road. (3) Suitable for local soil and water. (4) Rapid growth and great resistance. There are many tree species supplied to roadside trees. Among locust trees, plane trees, poplar trees, catalpa trees, large-leaf willows, and French plane trees, French plane trees, large-leaf willows, and locust trees are the easiest to grow. Therefore, this time, the above-mentioned several species are also designated as roadside trees. Its configuration method is to plant trees on all streets with a width of more than 15 meters, totaling about 109,700 meters, totaling about 32,020 plants. However, among the new plants, about 6,081 plants have already been planted. Therefore, excluding this number, 2939 plants should be planted on this road. According to this number of plants, how many should be planted each year, and how many years later this number can be completed, will depend on the street construction plan, and cannot be predetermined. For the convenience of calculation, the completion period is set to ten years, then about 2,600 plants should be planted each year. In addition, the number of plants replanted and renewed each year is calculated as one-tenth of the total number, then 320 plants in the first year, 3,460 plants in the second year, 3,720 plants in the third year, 3,984 plants in the fourth year, 4,240 plants in the fifth year, 4,500 plants in the sixth year, 4,760 plants in the seventh year, 5,020 plants in the eighth year, 5,380 plants in the ninth year, and 5,540 plants in the tenth year, totaling 43,700 plants. After that, 3,200 plants will be replanted and changed each year. As for its cost budget, according to the planting experience of the Engineering Bureau, including the cost of digging trees, packaging, transportation, digging holes, planting, and setting up new supports, it costs about one yuan to plant one tree. According to the previous ten years, the cost required for planting each year is 43,700 yuan.

Buick Ice Racing Record Ji Ren 195

Speeding at 100 Miles Per Hour

Winning the Mack's Silver Cup

Unprecedented Record

The north is bitterly cold, and ice skating is popular. This type of game is no longer very timely. New-style ice skating sports are now all replaced by car ice racing. The city of Nufo Shi Gao Tuo in Setterney, Canada, holds an ice race every year. This year, the winner of the Mack Ayatt Silver Cup was still the ice racer Dick Luo Ji and his company.

Every winter, the harbor surface accumulates ice a foot thick, which is firm and smooth, making it a natural runway. When the competition is held, men and women from the city and countryside rush to visit. The road to Shanyin is endless with traffic. The area is the most famous speedway in the world, and the results of each competition often break global records.

This year, Luo Ji and his company drove a new Buick racing car to join the competition, setting an unprecedented record. The runway was a saltwater river surface, starting from Edward and ending at Setterney. They sped away, with an average speed of 105.88 miles per hour, that is, 2.5 miles per minute and a half. At the fastest time, it could increase to more than 110 miles per hour.

As a result, the first to reach the finish line was Luo Ji and his company, driving a Buick, about three-quarters of a mile away from the second racing car. The speed was unprecedented. The audience was amazed. It is said that Luo Ji and his company have won the championship four times, especially this time is the most glorious. Buick racing cars are used in every competition, and victory is guaranteed. Today, people call Luo Ji and his company the King of Ice.

A wedge-shaped wind deflector is added in front of the Buick car box of Luo Ji and his company to reduce the resistance of the wind. The gear ratio is also changed to suit the highest speed. Therefore, the engine of this Buick is specially equipped and is different from ordinary machines.

The Mack Ayatt Silver Cup Race is one of the most valuable events in Canadian sports. Each time, the audience is crowded and extremely enthusiastic. During the competition, there must be a security team to strictly protect the crowd from crowding into the runway to avoid danger. The players have their own factions to support them, forming teams and shouting to encourage them. The fanaticism is beyond description. There are even those who gamble on this in the field, with varying amounts and huge wins and losses. During this year's competition, one or two players were jealous of Luo Ji and his company's skills, and a small number of latecomers requested a rematch. Luo Ji and his company generously agreed. As a result, he finally won the first place. It can be seen that Buick's contribution to the winners is definitely not comparable to ordinary vehicles.

On the day of the competition, the ice was very thick, and the wind was smooth, so the speed of each car was faster. Gordon Ilmen drove a light Chevrolet racing car, and the speed per hour could also reach 80 miles, and he finally won the fourth place.

This time, the speed of each car was really amazing to the audience. It is incomprehensible to be able to control the smooth ice surface at such a fast speed. After detailed inspection, it was found that the tires of each car were equipped with wide-headed short needles. When the wheels rotate, the needle tips stretch and contract from time to time. Even if the speed is increased to the extreme, there is no risk of overturning.

The next day, there was an unofficial competition. The ice suddenly melted one or two inches, and the deep part became almost a pool. When each car drove past, the ice flowers flew up like a heavy rain. The players and the audience could not avoid it, and their whole bodies were wet, which was comparable to after a shower. But in an instant, the car had gone several miles away, which is unimaginable. It is also an interesting story.

Foreign Friends Visit the Studebaker Factory Huang Yingdai 196

28,000 Visitors in 1929

According to what Mr. Honisbao, the manager of the Studebaker Car Factory, said, last year, the situation of people visiting the car factory set up by Studebaker in SOUTHBEND was unprecedented. In a year, people from far and near came to visit the factory, with a total of more than 2,000 people. It is a remarkable thing that there were representatives from 22 countries. Since the establishment of the factory, there have never been so many visitors. The number of people visiting the factory from all over the United States was 27,799, including 19,654 from Indiana, Illinois, and the interior, including 387 students. Those who came to visit the factory from the University of Zidan were there to visit the engineering in the factory. There were 119 people who came from Masari Province, and 232 from California. There were also many visitors from other places such as Michigan, Iowa, New York, Ohio, Pennsylvania, and Wisconsin. As for foreigners, there were 129 people, representing almost all countries in the world, from all over the Far East, such as Japan, India, Siam, Australia, New Zealand, the Philippines, Honolulu, and Brazil, Peru, and Canada, Cuba, South America, Central America, Mexico, Ireland, Germany, the Netherlands, Czechoslovakia, England, Switzerland, and the Panama Canal. The factory welcomes all visitors very much. Every Saturday and Sunday, special cars are opened to welcome visitors, and there are uniformed receptionists to guide the visitors in the factory. The buses opened by the factory travel back and forth from the main factory to the branch factory, and can be reached in two hours each time.
